             </div> 
             <p class="o-teaser__standfirst">President warns Congress: ‘I will never sign another bill like this again’</p> 
             <div class="o-teaser__timestamp"> 
              <time data-o-component="o-date" class="o-date" data-o-date-format="time-ago-limit-4-hours" datetime="2018-03-23T18:21:01.000Z">Friday, 23 March, 2018</time> 
             </div>
